    local function getCorners(p1, p2, p3) --[[ getCorners | Line: 48 ]]

    	for k, v in pairs(p3) do
    		local v1 = math.floor(v / 4) % 2 * 2 - 1

    local function getModelPointCloud(p1) --[[ getModelPointCloud | Line: 57 | Upvalues: t2 (copy), t3 (copy), t (copy), getCorners (copy) ]]
    	local t4 = {}
    	for k, v in pairs(p1:GetDescendants()) do
    		if v:IsA("BasePart") then
    			for k2, v3 in pairs((getCorners(v.CFrame, v.Size / 2, if v:IsA("WedgePart") then t2 elseif v:IsA("CornerWedgePart") then t3 else t))) do
    				table.insert(t4, v3)
    local function viewProjectionEdgeHits(p1, p2, p3, p4) --[[ viewProjectionEdgeHits | Line: 71 ]]
    	local v1 = (-1 / 0)
    	local v2 = (1 / 0)
    	for k, v in pairs(p1) do
    		local v3 = p4 * (p3 - v.Z)
    		local v4 = v[p2] + v3
    		local v5 = v[p2] - v3
    		local v6 = math.max(v1, v4, v5)
    		v1, v2 = v6, math.min(v2, v4, v5)
    function t4.new(p1, p2) --[[ new | Line: 90 | Upvalues: t4 (copy) ]]
    	local v2 = setmetatable({}, t4)
    	v2.Model = nil
    	v2.ViewportFrame = p1
    	v2.Camera = p2
    	v2._points = {}
    	v2._modelCFrame = CFrame.new()
    	v2._modelSize = Vector3.new()

    	v2._viewport = {}
    	v2:Calibrate()
    function t4.SetModel(p1, p2) --[[ SetModel | Line: 114 | Upvalues: getModelPointCloud (copy) ]]
    	p1.Model = p2
    	local v1, v2 = p2:GetBoundingBox()
    	p1._points = getModelPointCloud(p2)
    	p1._modelCFrame = v1
    	p1._modelSize = v2
    	p1._modelRadius = v2.Magnitude / 2
    function t4.Calibrate(p1) --[[ Calibrate | Line: 127 ]]
    	local t = {}
    	local AbsoluteSize = p1.ViewportFrame.AbsoluteSize
    	t.aspect = AbsoluteSize.X / AbsoluteSize.Y
    	t.yFov2 = math.rad(p1.Camera.FieldOfView / 2)
    	t.tanyFov2 = math.tan(t.yFov2)
    	t.xFov2 = math.atan(t.tanyFov2 * t.aspect)
    	t.tanxFov2 = math.tan(t.xFov2)
    	t.cFov2 = math.atan(t.tanyFov2 * math.min(1, t.aspect))
    	t.sincFov2 = math.sin(t.cFov2)
    	p1._viewport = t
    function t4.GetFitDistance(p1, p2) --[[ GetFitDistance | Line: 149 ]]
    	return (p1._modelRadius + (p2 and (p2 - p1._modelCFrame.Position).Magnitude or 0)) / p1._viewport.sincFov2
    function t4.GetMinimumFitCFrame(p1, p2) --[[ GetMinimumFitCFrame | Line: 161 | Upvalues: viewProjectionEdgeHits (copy) ]]
    	if p1.Model then
    		local v1 = (p2 - p2.Position):Inverse()
    		local _points = p1._points
    		local t = { v1 * _points[1] }
    		local Z = t[1].Z
    		for i = 2, #_points do
    			local v2 = v1 * _points[i]
    			local v3 = math.min(Z, v2.Z)
    			t[i] = v2
    			Z = v3
    		local v4, v5 = viewProjectionEdgeHits(t, "X", Z, p1._viewport.tanxFov2)
    		local v6, v7 = viewProjectionEdgeHits(t, "Y", Z, p1._viewport.tanyFov2)
    		return p2 * CFrame.new((v4 + v5) / 2, (v6 + v7) / 2, Z + math.max((v4 - v5) / 2 / p1._viewport.tanxFov2, (v6 - v7) / 2 / p1._viewport.tanyFov2))
    		return CFrame.new()
    return {
    	ViewportModelClass = t4
    }

  ik_solver (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.public.ik_solver
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    return function(p1, p2, p3, p4, p5, p6) --[[ solveIK | Line: 3 ]]
    	local v1 = p3:pointToObjectSpace(p4)
    	local Unit = v1.Unit
    	local Magnitude = v1.Magnitude
    	local v5 = p3 * CFrame.fromAxisAngle((Vector3.new(0, 0, -1)):Cross(Unit), (math.acos(-Unit.Z)))
    	if Magnitude < math.max(p6, p5) - math.min(p6, p5) then
    		return v5 * CFrame.new(0, 0, math.max(p6, p5) - math.min(p6, p5) - Magnitude), -1.5707963267948966, math.pi
    	elseif p5 + p6 < Magnitude then
    		return v5 * CFrame.new(0, 0, p5 + p6 - Magnitude), 1.5707963267948966, 0
    		local v6 = -math.acos((-(p6 * p6) + p5 * p5 + Magnitude * Magnitude) / (2 * p5 * Magnitude))
    		return v5, v6 + 1.5707963267948966, math.acos((p6 * p6 - p5 * p5 + Magnitude * Magnitude) / (2 * p6 * Magnitude)) - v6
    --- END CODE ---

    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---

    	use_reticle_display = true,
    	use_eye_relief = true,
    	is_aim_marker_fixed = true,
    	is_scope = true,
    	is_black_in_night_vision = true,
    	brightness = {
    		nv = 0.1,
    		default = 10
    	},
    	variable_magnification = {
    		default_zoom = 0,
    		offset = 0.9,
    		min_fov = 10,
    		max_fov = 50,
    		min_reticle_size = 1,
    		max_reticle_size = 9,
    		lever = function(p1) --[[ lever | Line: 24 ]]
